The architecture consists of three main layers:\\n\\n## Core Interface and Services\\n\\n**GroupCoordinator.java** (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinator.java) is the main interface defining the GroupCoordinator API with methods for joinGroup(), syncGroup(), and heartbeat() operations that handle classic consumer groups, modern consumer groups, share groups, and streams groups.\\n\\n**GroupCoordinatorService.java** and **GroupCoordinatorShard.java** provide the service and shard implementations that delegate to GroupMetadataManager for actual request processing.\\n\\n## State Machines\\n\\nThe codebase implements multiple state machines for different group types:\\n\\n1. **Classic Groups** - ClassicGroupState.java defines an enum with five states:\\n   - EMPTY: Group has no members but lingers until offset expiration\\n   - PREPARING_REBALANCE: Group is preparing to rebalance\\n   - COMPLETING_REBALANCE: Group is awaiting state assignment from leader\\n   - STABLE: Group is stable with assigned members\\n   - DEAD: Group metadata is being removed\\n\\n2. **Consumer Groups** - ConsumerGroup.java (in modern/consumer) defines ConsumerGroupState enum with states: EMPTY, ASSIGNING, RECONCILING, STABLE, DEAD\\n\\n3. **Share Groups** - ShareGroup.java (in modern/share) defines ShareGroupState enum with states: EMPTY, STABLE, DEAD, UNKNOWN\\n\\n4. **Streams Groups** - StreamsGroup.java (in streams) defines StreamsGroupState enum with states: EMPTY, NOT_READY, ASSIGNING, RECONCILING, STABLE, DEAD\\n\\n## Request Handlers\\n\\n**GroupMetadataManager.java** contains the implementation of JoinGroup and SyncGroup request handlers:\\n- classicGroupJoin() - Entry point for JoinGroup requests\\n- classicGroupJoinToClassicGroup() - Routes new or existing classic groups\\n- classicGroupJoinNewMember() - Handles new member joins\\n- classicGroupJoinExistingMember() - Handles existing member rejoins\\n- syncGroup() - Handles SyncGroup requests from group members\\n\\nThese methods manage state transitions and coordinate the rebalancing protocol between JoinGroup and SyncGroup phases.\\n\\n## Heartbeat Expiry Detection\\n\\n**Heartbeat expiry detection** is implemented in GroupMetadataManager.java through:\\n- expireClassicGroupMemberHeartbeat() - Invoked when heartbeat operation expires from timer. Checks if member has satisfied recent heartbeat requirement and removes member from group if heartbeat has expired\\n- rescheduleClassicGroupMemberHeartbeat() - Manages scheduling of periodic heartbeat expiration checks using CoordinatorTimer\\n- ClassicGroupMember tracks sessionTimeoutMs and rebalanceTimeoutMs for detecting timeouts\\n\\nThe heartbeat expiry mechanism detects member failures and triggers state transitions:\\n- If a member in STABLE state fails heartbeat, group transitions to PREPARING_REBALANCE\\n- If all members in PREPARING_REBALANCE have joined by timeout, group transitions to COMPLETING_REBALANCE\\n- Members with expired heartbeats are removed from the group\\n\\n## Member Metadata\\n\\n**ClassicGroupMember.java** holds member metadata including:\\n- memberId and groupInstanceId (for static membership)\\n- sessionTimeoutMs and rebalanceTimeoutMs for heartbeat tracking\\n- awaitingJoinFuture and awaitingSyncFuture for async coordination\\n\\n**ModernGroupMember.java** (and subclasses ConsumerGroupMember, ShareGroupMember, StreamsGroupMember) provide modern group member implementations with MemberState tracking (STABLE, UNREVOKED_PARTITIONS, UNRELEASED_PARTITIONS).\\n\\nThe GroupCoordinator implementation handles all aspects of group membership management, state machine transitions, rebalancing protocol execution, and failure detection through heartbeat expiry mechanisms.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":10,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1650,"cache_read_input_tokens":67345,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1650},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"252cdd7f-9534-47c1-947d-554dcb4077c6","uuid":"6d2502b8-f30e-404b-aa48-39b055722acc"}

The architecture consists of three main layers:\\n\\n## Core Interface and Services\\n\\n**GroupCoordinator.java** (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinator.java) is the main interface defining the GroupCoordinator API with methods for joinGroup(), syncGroup(), and heartbeat() operations that handle classic consumer groups, modern consumer groups, share groups, and streams groups.\\n\\n**GroupCoordinatorService.java** and **GroupCoordinatorShard.java** provide the service and shard implementations that delegate to GroupMetadataManager for actual request processing.\\n\\n## State Machines\\n\\nThe codebase implements multiple state machines for different group types:\\n\\n1. **Classic Groups** - ClassicGroupState.java defines an enum with five states:\\n   - EMPTY: Group has no members but lingers until offset expiration\\n   - PREPARING_REBALANCE: Group is preparing to rebalance\\n   - COMPLETING_REBALANCE: Group is awaiting state assignment from leader\\n   - ShareGroup.java (in modern/share) defines ShareGroupState enum with states: EMPTY, STABLE, DEAD, UNKNOWN\\n\\n4. **Streams Groups** - StreamsGroup.java (in streams) defines StreamsGroupState enum with states: EMPTY, NOT_READY, ASSIGNING, RECONCILING, STABLE, DEAD\\n\\n## Request Handlers\\n\\n**GroupMetadataManager.java** contains the implementation of JoinGroup and SyncGroup request handlers:\\n- classicGroupJoin() - Entry point for JoinGroup requests\\n- classicGroupJoinToClassicGroup() - Routes new or existing classic groups\\n- classicGroupJoinNewMember() - Handles new member joins\\n- classicGroupJoinExistingMember() - Handles existing member rejoins\\n- syncGroup() - Handles SyncGroup requests from group members\\n\\nThese methods manage state transitions and coordinate the rebalancing protocol between JoinGroup and SyncGroup phases.\\n\\n## Heartbeat Expiry Detection\\n\\n**Heartbeat expiry detection** is implemented in GroupMetadataManager.java through:\\n- expireClassicGroupMemberHeartbeat() - Invoked when heartbeat operation expires from timer. Checks if member has satisfied recent heartbeat requirement and removes member from group if heartbeat has expired\\n- rescheduleClassicGroupMemberHeartbeat() - Manages scheduling of periodic heartbeat expiration checks using CoordinatorTimer\\n- ClassicGroupMember tracks sessionTimeoutMs and rebalanceTimeoutMs for detecting timeouts\\n\\nThe heartbeat expiry mechanism detects member failures and triggers state transitions:\\n- If a member in STABLE state fails heartbeat, group transitions to PREPARING_REBALANCE\\n- If all members in PREPARING_REBALANCE have joined by timeout, group transitions to COMPLETING_REBALANCE\\n- Members with expired heartbeats are removed from the group\\n\\n## Member Metadata\\n\\n**ClassicGroupMember.java** holds member metadata including:\\n- memberId and groupInstanceId (for static membership)\\n- sessionTimeoutMs and rebalanceTimeoutMs for heartbeat tracking\\n- awaitingJoinFuture and awaitingSyncFuture for async coordination\\n\\n**ModernGroupMember.java** (and subclasses ConsumerGroupMember, ShareGroupMember, StreamsGroupMember) provide modern group member implementations with MemberState tracking (STABLE, UNREVOKED_PARTITIONS, UNRELEASED_PARTITIONS).\\n\\nThe GroupCoordinator implementation handles all aspects of group membership management, state machine transitions, rebalancing protocol execution, and failure detection through heartbeat expiry mechanisms.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
